##########################################################################################################
############################## Vendor Application Database Queries #######################################
##########################################################################################################

-- Roles
CREATE TABLE roles(
role_id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY NOT NULL,
role_name character varying (15),
role_description character varying (55),
active boolean DEFAULT true NOT NULL,
isDeleted boolean DEFAULT false NOT NULL,
createddate timestamp without time zone DEFAULT ('now'::text)::date NOT NULL,
lastmodifieddate timestamp without time zone
)

 -- Users
CREATE TABLE users(
user_id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY NOT NULL,
firstname character varying (50) NOT NULL,
lastname character varying (50) NOT NULL,
username character varying (50) NOT NULL unique,
password character varying (50),
mobile_number INTEGER NOT NULL,
age INTEGER NOT NULL,
email character varying(100),
gender_id INTEGER,
p_address character varying(255),
c_address character varying(255),
active boolean DEFAULT true NOT NULL,
isDeleted boolean DEFAULT false NOT NULL,
createddate timestamp without time zone DEFAULT ('now'::text)::date,
updatedDate timestamp without time zone ,
lastmodifieddate timestamp without time zone,
FOREIGN KEY (gender_id) REFERENCES gender(gender_id)
);





-- Role Mapping
CREATE TABLE user_role_mapping(
id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY NOT NULL,
user_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
role_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
active boolean DEFAULT true NOT NULL,
createddate timestamp without time zone DEFAULT ('now'::text)::date NOT NULL,
lastmodifieddate timestamp without time zone
FOREIGN KEY (user_id) REFERENCES users(user_id),
FOREIGN KEY (role_id) REFERENCES roles(role_id)

)



-- gender Table
CREATE TABLE gender(
     gender_id serial PRIMARY KEY NOT NULL,
     gender_name character varying(50) NOT NULL,
     active boolean DEFAULT true NOT NULL,
     createddate timestamp without time zone DEFAULT ('now'::text)::date NOT NULL,
     lastmodifieddate timestamp with time zone
);

INSERT INTO gender ( gender_name, active) VALUES ('Male' ,true);
INSERT INTO gender ( gender_name, active) VALUES ('Female' ,true);
INSERT INTO gender ( gender_name, active) VALUES ('Other' ,true);


CREATE TABLE mst_nationality (
    nationality_id serial PRIMARY KEY  NOT NULL,
    nationality_name character varying(50) NOT NULL,
    active boolean DEFAULT true NOT NULL,
    createddate timestamp without time zone DEFAULT ('now'::text)::date NOT NULL,
    lastmodifieddate timestamp without time zone
);
INSERT INTO mst_nationality ( nationality_name, active) VALUES ('Indian' ,true);
INSERT INTO mst_nationality ( nationality_name, active) VALUES ('Nepali' ,true);
INSERT INTO mst_nationality ( nationality_name, active) VALUES ('Other' ,true);


CREATE TABLE mst_vendor (
    ventype_id serial PRIMARY KEY  NOT NULL,
    ventype_name character varying(50) NOT NULL,
    active boolean DEFAULT true NOT NULL,
    createddate timestamp without time zone DEFAULT ('now'::text)::date NOT NULL,
    lastmodifieddate timestamp without time zone
);
INSERT INTO mst_vendor ( ventype_name, active) VALUES ('Stationary' ,true);
INSERT INTO mst_vendor ( ventype_name, active) VALUES ('Movable' ,true);



-- State
CREATE TABLE mst_state (
    state_id serial PRIMARY KEY  NOT NULL,
    state_name character varying(100) NOT NULL,
    is_active boolean DEFAULT true NOT NULL,
    is_deleted boolean DEFAULT false NOT NULL,
    created_on timestamp without time zone DEFAULT ('now'::text)::date NOT NULL
);

--- District
CREATE TABLE mst_district (
    district_id serial PRIMARY KEY  NOT NULL,
    district_name character varying(100) NOT NULL,
    state_id Integer NOT NULL,
    alert_zone character varying(50),
    is_active boolean DEFAULT true NOT NULL,
    is_deleted boolean DEFAULT false NOT NULL,
    created_on timestamp without time zone DEFAULT ('now'::text)::date NOT NULL,
    FOREIGN KEY (state_id) REFERENCES mst_state(state_id)

);

--- Block
CREATE TABLE mst_block (
    block_id serial PRIMARY KEY  NOT NULL,
    block_name character varying(100) NOT NULL,
    block_code Integer NOT NULL,
    district_id Integer NOT NULL,
    is_active boolean DEFAULT true NOT NULL,
    is_deleted boolean DEFAULT false NOT NULL,
    created_on timestamp without time zone DEFAULT ('now'::text)::date NOT NULL,
    FOREIGN KEY (district_id) REFERENCES mst_district(district_id)

);

CREATE TABLE mst_sub_division (
    sub_div_id serial PRIMARY KEY  NOT NULL,
    subdivision_name character varying(100) NOT NULL,
    district_id Integer NOT NULL,
    is_active boolean DEFAULT true NOT NULL,
    is_deleted boolean DEFAULT false NOT NULL,
    FOREIGN KEY (district_id) REFERENCES mst_district(district_id)
);

CREATE TABLE mst_tehsil (
    tehsil_id serial PRIMARY KEY  NOT NULL,
    tehsil_name character varying(100) NOT NULL,
    district_id Integer NOT NULL,
    sub_division_id Integer NOT NULL,
    created_on timestamp without time zone DEFAULT ('now'::text)::date NOT NULL,
    is_active boolean DEFAULT true NOT NULL,
    is_deleted boolean DEFAULT false NOT NULL,
    Tehsildar Integer,
    SDM Integer,
    FOREIGN KEY (district_id) REFERENCES mst_district(district_id)
);

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `mst_gram_panchyat`;


-- mst_gram_panchyat
CREATE TABLE mst_gram_panchyat (
    panchayat_id serial PRIMARY KEY  NOT NULL,
    panchayat_name character varying(100) NOT NULL,
    pachayat_code Integer NOT NULL,
    block_id Integer NOT NULL,
    bo_block_id Integer NOT NULL,
    panchayat_pradhan_number Integer DEFAULT NULL,
    created_on timestamp without time zone DEFAULT ('now'::text)::date NOT NULL,
    is_active boolean DEFAULT true NOT NULL,
    is_deleted boolean DEFAULT false NOT NULL,
    panchayat_secretary_number Integer,
    type character varying(20) DEFAULT NULL,
    district_name character varying(100) DEFAULT NULL,
    FOREIGN KEY (block_id) REFERENCES mst_block(block_id)
);

CREATE TABLE mst_vendortype (
    vendortype_id serial PRIMARY KEY  NOT NULL,
    ventype_id Integer NOT NULL,
    vendortype_name character varying(50) NOT NULL,
    active boolean DEFAULT true NOT NULL,
    createddate timestamp without time zone DEFAULT ('now'::text)::date NOT NULL,
    lastmodifieddate timestamp without time zone,
    FOREIGN KEY (venType_id) REFERENCES mst_vendor(venType_id)
);
INSERT INTO mst_vendortype ( ventype_id,vendortype_name,active) VALUES (1, 'Tent' ,true);
INSERT INTO mst_vendortype ( ventype_id,vendortype_name,active) VALUES (1, 'Food Van' ,true);
INSERT INTO mst_vendortype ( ventype_id,vendortype_name,active) VALUES (1, 'Dhaba' ,true);
INSERT INTO mst_vendortype ( ventype_id,vendortype_name,active) VALUES (1, 'Clothing Shop' ,true);
INSERT INTO mst_vendortype ( ventype_id,vendortype_name,active) VALUES (2, 'Photographers' ,true);
INSERT INTO mst_vendortype ( ventype_id,vendortype_name,active) VALUES (2, 'Chai Hawkers' ,true);




CREATE TABLE mst_district (
    district_id serial PRIMARY KEY  NOT NULL,
    district_name character varying(50) NOT NULL,
    active boolean DEFAULT true NOT NULL,
    createddate timestamp without time zone DEFAULT ('now'::text)::date NOT NULL,
    lastmodifieddate timestamp without time zone
);
INSERT INTO mst_district ( district_name, active) VALUES ('Lahaul' ,true);
INSERT INTO mst_district ( district_name, active) VALUES ('Spiti' ,true);


CREATE TABLE mst_areaavailable (
    area_id serial PRIMARY KEY  NOT NULL,
    area_name character varying(50) NOT NULL,
    district_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
    active boolean DEFAULT true NOT NULL,
    createddate timestamp without time zone DEFAULT ('now'::text)::date NOT NULL,
    lastmodifieddate timestamp without time zone,
    FOREIGN KEY (district_id) REFERENCES mst_district(district_id)
);

CREATE TABLE user_application (
    app_id serial PRIMARY KEY  NOT NULL,
    user_id Integer NOT NULL,
    nationality_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
    ventype_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
    vendortype_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
    tent_number INTEGER,
    district_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
    identity_doc character varying(255) NOT NULL,
    app_action_dc character varying(1) NOT NULL,  -- P,A,R
    dc_comments character varying(255),
    app_action_dfo character varying(1),
    dfo_comments character varying(255),
    app_action_bdo character varying(1),
    bdo_comments character varying(255),
    vendor_comments character varying(255),
    active boolean DEFAULT true NOT NULL,
    createddate timestamp without time zone DEFAULT ('now'::text)::date NOT NULL,
    lastmodifieddate timestamp without time zone,
    FOREIGN KEY (user_id) REFERENCES users(user_id),
    FOREIGN KEY (nationality_id) REFERENCES mst_nationality(nationality_id),
    FOREIGN KEY (ventype_id) REFERENCES mst_vendor(ventype_id),
    FOREIGN KEY (vendortype_id) REFERENCES mst_vendortype(vendortype_id),
    FOREIGN KEY (district_id) REFERENCES mst_district(district_id)
);
ALTER TABLE user_application ADD COLUMN app_bdo_date timestamp without time zone;
ALTER TABLE user_application ADD COLUMN app_dfo_date timestamp without time zone;
ALTER TABLE user_application ADD COLUMN app_dc_date timestamp without time zone;


CREATE TABLE routs (
    id serial PRIMARY KEY  NOT NULL,
    app_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
    area_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
    active boolean DEFAULT true NOT NULL,
    createddate timestamp without time zone DEFAULT ('now'::text)::date NOT NULL,
    lastmodifieddate timestamp without time zone,
    FOREIGN KEY (app_id) REFERENCES user_application(app_id),
    FOREIGN KEY (area_id) REFERENCES mst_areaavailable(area_id)
);


--Transaction Table
CREATE TABLE user_transaction (
    id serial PRIMARY KEY  NOT NULL,
    app_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
    email character varying(100),
    name character varying(100),
    phone character varying(100),
    amount character varying(50),
    payment_Status character varying(10),
    transaction_id character varying(200) UNIQUE,
    mihpay_id character varying (200) UNIQUE,
    payment_mode character varying (10),
    bank_ref_number character varying(150),
    error character varying(255),
    active boolean DEFAULT true NOT NULL,
    paymentdate timestamp without time zone DEFAULT ('now'::text)::date NOT NULL,
    paymentdateresponse timestamp without time zone DEFAULT ('now'::text)::date NOT NULL

);


-- OTP TABLE
CREATE TABLE otp_logs (
    id serial PRIMARY KEY  NOT NULL,
    app_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
    phone character varying(100),
    sent_message character varying(255),
    cdac_response character varying(255),
    send_time timestamp without time zone DEFAULT ('now'::text)::date NOT NULL
);

-- User Form Data
CREATE TABLE userFormData (
    user_id serial PRIMARY KEY  NOT NULL,
    user_type_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
    reservationtype_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
    full_name character varying(50) NOT NULL,
    relationshipprifix_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
    relation_name character varying(50) NOT NULL,
    mobile_number INTEGER NOT NULL,
    age INTEGER NOT NULL,
    weight INTEGER NOT NULL,
    luggage_weight INTEGER NOT NULL,
    p_address character varying(255) NOT NULL,
    c_address character varying(255) ,
    reasonavailing_flight_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
    comments character varying(255),
    tentitive_flight_date character varying(10) NOT NULL ,
    availed_flight_befor15 character varying(2) NOT NULL ,
    earlier_flight_service_emergency character varying(2) NOT NULL ,
    decleration_user character varying(2) NOT NULL ,
    district_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
    helipad_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
	district_id_dest INTEGER NOT NULL,
    helipad_id_dest INTEGER NOT NULL,
    earlierService character varying(2) NOT NULL,
    aadhaar_doc_name character varying(100),
    office_card_coc_name character varying(100),
    medical_doc_name character varying(100),
    other_doc character varying(100),
    role_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
    application_status character varying(2) NOT NULL,
    concerned_authority_comments character varying(255),
    is_boarded character varying(10),
    boarded_comments character varying(255),
    tentitive_flight_date_to character varying(25),
    active boolean DEFAULT true NOT NULL,
    createddate timestamp with time zone DEFAULT ('now'::text)::date ,
    lastmodifieddate timestamp without time zone,
    FOREIGN KEY (user_type_id) REFERENCES mst_typeuser(user_type_id),
    FOREIGN KEY (reservationtype_id) REFERENCES mst_reservationtype(reservationtype_id),
    FOREIGN KEY (relationshipprifix_id) REFERENCES mst_relationshipprefix(relationshipprifix_id),
    FOREIGN KEY (reasonavailing_flight_id) REFERENCES mst_reasonavailing_flight(reasonavailing_flight_id),
    FOREIGN KEY (district_id) REFERENCES mst_district(district_id),
    FOREIGN KEY (helipad_id) REFERENCES mst_helipad(helipad_id),
    FOREIGN KEY (role_id) REFERENCES roles(role_id),
	FOREIGN KEY (district_id_dest) REFERENCES mst_district_dest(district_id_dest),
    FOREIGN KEY (helipad_id_dest) REFERENCES mst_helipad_dest(helipad_id_dest)

);

ALTER TABLE  userFormData ADD COLUMN concerned_authority_comments character varying (255);


-- Indexing Goes Here
CREATE INDEX idx_userFormData_user_id ON userFormData USING btree (user_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_userFormData_mobile_number ON userFormData USING btree (mobile_number);
CREATE INDEX idx_userFormData_age ON userFormData USING btree (age);
CREATE INDEX idx_userFormData_district_id ON userFormData USING btree (district_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_userFormData_helipad_id ON userFormData USING btree (helipad_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_userFormData_full_name ON userFormData USING btree (full_name);


-- userFormData_previousService
CREATE TABLE userFormData_previousService (
    id serial PRIMARY KEY  NOT NULL,
    user_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
    date character varying(100) ,
    district_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
    helipad_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
    active boolean DEFAULT true NOT NULL,
    createddate timestamp without time zone DEFAULT ('now'::text)::date NOT NULL,
    lastmodifieddate timestamp without time zone,
    FOREIGN KEY (user_id) REFERENCES userformdata(user_id),
    FOREIGN KEY (district_id) REFERENCES mst_district(district_id),
    FOREIGN KEY (helipad_id) REFERENCES mst_helipad(helipad_id)
);
